   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Press Freedom Index</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p class="mw-empty-elt"> </p> 
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Reporters Without Borders assessment of countries' press freedom
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Press_freedom_2020.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Press_freedom_2020.svg/400px-Press_freedom_2020.svg.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="203" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Press_freedom_2020.svg/600px-Press_freedom_2020.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Press_freedom_2020.svg/800px-Press_freedom_2020.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="3494" data-file-height="1772"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Press_freedom_2020.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>2020 Press Freedom Index</b><sup id="cite_ref-:0_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-1">[1]</a></sup> 
         <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style>
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#005f9a; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Good situation
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#8eb0d6; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Satisfactory situation
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ffb035; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Noticeable problems
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ff3022; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Difficult situation
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#83000b; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Very serious situation
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#dcdcdc; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Not classified
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The <b>Press Freedom Index</b> is an annual ranking of countries compiled and published by <a href="/wiki/Reporters_Without_Borders" title="Reporters Without Borders">Reporters Without Borders</a> based upon the organisation's own assessment of the countries' <a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_the_press" title="Freedom of the press">press freedom</a> records in the previous year. It intends to reflect the degree of freedom that <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalists</a>, news organisations, and <a href="/wiki/Netizens" class="mw-redirect" title="Netizens">netizens</a> have in each country, and the efforts made by authorities to respect this <a href="/wiki/Freedom" title="Freedom">freedom</a>. Reporters Without Borders is careful to note that the index only deals with press freedom and does not measure the quality of journalism nor does it look at <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> violations in general.<sup id="cite_ref-RWBPFIHow_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RWBPFIHow-2">[2]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The report is partly based on a questionnaire<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> using six general criteria: pluralism (measures the degree of representation of opinions in the media space), <a href="/wiki/Media_independence" title="Media independence">media independence</a>, environment and <a href="/wiki/Self-censorship" title="Self-censorship">self-censorship</a>, legislative framework, transparency, and infrastructure. The questionnaire takes account of the legal framework for the media (including penalties for press offences, the existence of a <a href="/wiki/State_monopoly" title="State monopoly">state monopoly</a> for certain kinds of media and how the media are regulated) and the level of independence of the public media. It also includes violations of the free flow of information on the <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a>. </p>
      <p>Violence against journalists, netizens, and media assistants, including abuses attributable to the state, armed militias, clandestine organisations or pressure groups, are monitored by RSF staff during the year and are also part of the final score. A smaller score on the report corresponds to greater freedom of the press as reported by the organisation. The questionnaire is sent to Reporters Without Borders's partner organisations: 18 freedom of expression non-governmental organisations located in five continents, its 150 correspondents around the world and journalists, researchers, jurists and human rights activists.<sup id="cite_ref-RWBPFIHow_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RWBPFIHow-2">[2]</a></sup> </p>
